< review>
This place is epic!!! The guys at Riverside Archery have an answer for every question dealing with archery. They can get a hold of any bow within a reasonable time period, if they don't have it on the shelf. Mostly all work done on a bow is already quoted for. There is no hourly fee for tuning a bow like some places I have been too. Shooting on the range is always fun and the people I have met are so nice. Customer service is their #1 goal. They have lessons for all ages and skill levels which is great for a family or for the competitive archer.</review>

< Review>
Without a doubt THE place to go for anything archery-related in the Inland Empire. The variety of products, and their knowledge, is vast. In fact, I would advise anyone in Los Angeles to venture out here for their archery needs. Speak to Ian, he's the guy that took care of me and gave me a ton of advice and re-sized my arrows to just the right length. He signed me up for a range card, which is free and necessary to clock in and out with when using their indoor range. They start you off with a free $7 credit (equivalent to 1 hour range time) and you get another one on your birthday. Since my birthday was the day prior, Ian still gave it to me, so I started off with 2 free hours of range time on my card. This is awesome because I typically have time to kill after work waiting for traffic to die down. Like I stated, their service is awesome.

My only reason for not giving it a 5-star rating is that while Ian was working on my arrows, the news was on the TV and the president came on. One of the other staff members just couldn't hold in his personal opinions to himself and felt the need to shout them out to no one in particular (that was a bit weird). Regardless of any political leanings you may or may not have, this is just not professional, as it can be offensive to some. Not a deal-breaker, I'll still be going back, just an irksome moment in an otherwise perfect customer service experience.< /Review>

< Text>
I have been to this store 3 times. First two trips were fact finding tours. These guys are great. First time I went on a Monday (they were closed) but Ian and Travis saw me out there and came out to talk with me and answered a lot of my questions. I am a beginner as in never shot before.

Second Trip, I came back from visiting a few other archery stores in the Orange county area and thought I had some idea of what I wanted. Bernie let me try out bows from beginning to advanced. Answered questions and gave me some shooting tips. At no point during any of this did they pressure me to buy or give many anything less that excellent service. I was there a few hours and did not purchase a thing.

Third trip I had nailed it down and once again wanted to shoot to particular bows for comparison. They again were very happy to help. This time I was being helped by Evan. I asked to shoot both bows on the range to have a further target and the obliged. I had made a choice. Of course I changed it the next day and finally placed the order.

4th Trip is today to pick up my bow and get accessories as well as shoot it. I will post another review to let you all know how today went, but I expect I will be satisfied as these guys have been great during this entire process. The just want me to be really happy with my purchase and archery as a whole.</Text>

<review>Read the reviews on here and I was a little skeptical at first. But, they were the only remotely close pro shop that had the bow I wanted in stock in the finish I wanted, so I called them on Saturday and had them hold it for me until I could go there the following Tuesday. So I made the 75 mile drive from Carlsbad. The area wasn't so enticing but it wasn't bad. Once they opened I was immediately helped while the worker started setting up for the day. I told them I was new, it was my first bow, and that they were supposed to be holding a bow for me. He new exactly what I was talking about and brought it out. As he took out the bow, he asked another customer what he needed. The other customer needed something fixed and it wouldn't take that long. I let the worker go ahead and start taking care of the other customer. At that point, the owner's son, Travis, came in. He took over helping me out from there. They measured my draw length and determined that the bow was already set for my draw length. Even then, Travis proceeded to re-Loctite all the screws on the Cams for me while showing me all the spots of the bow to keep an eye on and how to check them. After re-inspecting the bow to make sure everything looked good, he reset the draw weight, aligned the rest, grabbed some arrows and explained how to adjust the sight. He stayed with me and let me adjust my own sight to ensure I did it correctly. While I was sighting it in, he was giving me a crash course lesson on how to improve my stance and shot. By the time I finished adjusting me sights, I was shooting a 2-2.5" group dead center at 20 yards.
At that point, he showed me all the things I would need or would want to buy/replace. He was never pushy on getting me to buy anything, which is big for me.
I think another thing I noticed was that he was still professional and helpful regardless of the fact that he knew I wasn't from the area, and probably wouldn't be giving  much of my business.
Overall, if they were closer this would be my main place to go, but unfortunately that's not the case. I'm sure I'll still drop by on my way to Vegas.
Great shop with great guys and a nicer selection compared to what I've seen in southern california.< /review>< Pictures>

<Review>It's been 25 years since I've touched a bow last.  Out of nowhere my beautiful wife says that she wants to give archery a try.  I was floored.  So we head over to Riverside Archery to check out what they had to offer.  The store was surprisingly busy for a Tuesday afternoon but still, we were greeted by Travis, the owner, who gave us almost two hours of his time picking out the right bows and personally adjusting them for us.  It took a couple of tries but he got it JUST RIGHT.  They have an archery range there within the store too and so they (Travis and Chris)  taught us how to shoot them properly.

About the store... archery is the only thing they do.  Their selection of bows ranges from the inexpensive to the very expensive ($1400) + used.  They have every accessory you can imagine and it is well staffed.  Everyone we came in contact with was ridiculously  helpful and enthusiastic about their jobs.  Travis was the stand-out among them but I also really liked Chris.

We ended up spending more than I expected but I did so happily.  If you haven't shot a bow in a while then it's worth checking out.  I did a lot of research before I bought.  After many wasted hours online I came to realize that this is not the kind of thing you can buy off eBay or at an online store.  You really need to be measured for your bow and have them adjust it so that the draw weight is comfortable.  I didn't expect to buy a Bowtech bow today but I followed their recommendations and am super pleased and can't wait to go out and play with my new toy.< /Review><Pics>None<//Pics><resp>None< /resp><gmapID>0x80dcb210ee367a23:0x47fc4d1425881e24</gmapID></record></dataset><record>

< text>
I'm honestly shocked to see ANY of these bad reviews, and I would love nothing more that to slap the whiney babies that talk down this GREAT shop!

Both my girlfriend and I are new to archery, and after months of searching for the perfect bow both online and in personal tests, I decided on a Bowtech, the only problem is, Riverside archery were the only ones that had it is stock! So, I drove 2 hours both ways from Ventura county to find my perfect bow.

I can't say enough how pleased I was when I got there, NEVER was I treated like an amateur (and being a macho male, I tend to feel that way easily in new environments), NEVER was I talked down to, and NEVER did I or my girlfriend feel uncomfortable at any point being in the store. Not only did both the owner and his son treat us with GRADE A service, but fellow patrons using the archery range with years of experience made me feel at home by sharing stories, adding shooting tips, and making us both feel confident in our beginning levels.

Overall, both of us were super happy leaving the store, I got my bow, and my girlfriend had her eyes opened to different shooting choices that she never considered (We almost left owning two bows, until I convinced her to cool her jets). I give these guys a 10/10, and only wish they were closer to my home, I'd go shooting there every day if I could. The few hours of them teaching and instructing, was more productive than the MONTH I've been going to archery clubs on the weekend.

If you have a stick up your A#$ and like to make bad reviews, pull it out, sharpen it, add some feathers, and shoot it from a bow at Riverside Archery, you won't regret it!<//text>

<Rate>1< /Rate><Text>Beware, this place is terrible. No air conditioning and many of the rooms have no windows so expect to bake during the summer. The elevator is narrow and often broke. There is usually trash left around the front door which is sometimes left propped open by tenants without a key so anyone could wander in. The entire place sometimes smells like sewage.
The back parking lot of the building seems to be favored by locals for illicit activities. Either for drug deals or a fight club, it's unknown but most nights, a run down car will be sitting by the side of the building as a "look out" with access to the back roped off for their crew. Having made the mistake of parking back there earlier in the day, you do not want to be stuck with your car left amongst these guys at night when they are operating.
Overall this is a dirty, shady place which is overpriced. You can find cheaper, cleaner and better rehearsal studios elsewhere in LA.< /Text>< Pics>

<name>Robyn Thomas< /name>< Review>
Finally a Thai restaurant in Riverside that serves genuine fresh Thai spring rolls (could use a bit more lemony basil) but otherwise awesome. Pay the extra for fresh shrimp x2. You get 3 pcs rolls per order and they were big! Satay was good, not dry with perfect peanut sauce and really good cucumber sauce.

They also offer common Chinese cuisine including orange chicken - tender, fresh and not over candied.

We did not love the chicken teriyaki was so so.

All and all, good quality,quantity. A bit pricey but I have paid as much for awful food. This is really good

Used Grubhub, from Oder to delivery (hot) 38 miniutes! And accurate (so rare).

Thanks!!!
Robyn</Review>

<userid>112500009141705216957< /userid>< Rate>
5</Rate>
<pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNmoY5lOiiN_2e6KUX6kpKpMGjm1uM2xYd8yG8i=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNXIGasJBVoqmXVXLLig2albHmr7T25bdKsCRTe=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]< /pictures>< text>
For me, the biggest reason this place gets 5 stars (besides the delicious food) is the cleanliness. I chatted with the cashier and she mentioned how much the owner likes to keep the place clean, and it shows. The dining area was practically spotless and the staff cleaned up as soon as a mess was present. Typically, hole-in-the-wall places can look pretty sloppy or dusty, but not here. If cleanliness is your jam, I recommend here for sure.

Now, onto the food. I got the Shrimp a la Diabla Burrito because I love spicy, but oh man that is a spicy burrito, even for me. I still loved it and it was delicious, but just a warning to make sure you can handle your spice before you bite into one of those. Also, I can't go to a Mexican restaurant without sampling their fish tacos and this one was no exception. One of the best fish tacos I've tried. Try the variety of their salsas too.

I definitely can't wait to go back here next time I'm down in San Diego.<//text>

<Rating>4< /Rating><Name>Chris Van Voorst</Name>< Text>
5 stars for excellent service, clean location, large portions and good prices.  3 stars for a bland, mediocre California burrito.

The restaurant was clean and well maintained, and the service was fast, friendly and polite.  The prices were good, and the chips and salsa were good quality.  My California burrito was hot and fresh, and it contained a large portion of underseasoned carne asada.  The tortilla was excellent.

I prefer crispy fries on my CA burrito, so I was disappointed that the fries were soft.  Guacamole was included at no extra charge, but it was bland.  There was queso instead of cheese, and it was also bland.</Text>

His salesmanship was fantastic, he welcomed me into the store, asked if I was looking for anything in particular, when I mentioned sunglasses, he showed me where to look for the different styles. He asked if I wanted polarized glasses, and when I answered "yes" he told me the pair I wanted didn't come polarized, but I could custom order them if I wanted, and I did. He was super cool and led me through the custom order process. My new sunglasses will be delivered to my house in the next couple weeks, and I couldn't be happier or more excited. Thank you so much Jeremy and Oakley, I can't wait to get them.< /review>

< text>
If I were on a deserted Island with only 1 restaurant to go to for the rest of my life, Mezzo would be the one. It is my dream girl of restaurants. Checks all my boxes and makes me feel both good and satisfied.

Our journey began years ago, when I was a young impressionable freshman in Berkeley. Every Wednesday I would get a chef salad after class and eat it for both my lunch and dinner. The portion was big enough that it could sustain even a growing boy like myself for two whole meals. The heartiness provided me comfort through countless disappointing test results, breakups, and failures. And the fact that it was primarily salad meant I didn't gain a single pound for it!

Bur if you're not into salad, their soup and sandwiches are also super yummy. Pretty much anything you get, you can try a sample beforehand. Make sure you take advantage of that if you have a hard time deciding. Regardless of how long the line is, the salaristas will make sure you get something you'll enjoy very much. 10/10. Highly recommended!

Fair warning: If you fall for this place, you may lose some friends. I have gotten more than a few horrified looks when I mention that my favorite restaurant in the whole wide world is a salad spot.< /text>

< rating>
5</rating>
< Text>
A really cool, easily accessible, trendy spot in downtown Berkeley with excellent, organic foods!

I've lived in the Bay all my life but this was my first time actually coming to Mezzo. It's a lot of fun - it toes the line of casual but a little nicer too. Not to make a crude comparison, but it goes for a Chipotle vibe, just trendier and more original.

This place has a TON of seating - it was way more spacious than I could have expected with a lot of fun outdoor seating areas and open-air indoor seating too. Very communal type of seating arrangement and it seemed like everyone was having a really good time. Even when it's crowded it's not difficult to find somewhere to sit.

The food here is really quite phenomenal, you can tell it's all naturally sourced and fresh-made when you order. At a little above average price point for a casual meal, this is definitely a place I would stop at again in Berkeley if you have a group that just wants to get some really good salads and sandwiches.</Text>

< review>
If you were visiting Berkeley, you need to try out caf√© Mezzo. You can get a great big bowl of delicious leafy greens mixed with your choice of poppyseed to their homemade green goddess dressing. The salad has a delicious mixture of croutons, avocado, cherry tomatoes, beans, an egg and my favorite the sprouts. It‚Äôs a beautiful and healthy masterpiece when they prepare it. You always get a side of this hearty piece of bread with your salad and it‚Äôs also used for the sandwiches.
If you really love the bread, Mezzo sells bags of bread ends for buck.

Mezzo also provides options of sandwiches as well as soups. One of my favorite things about this place as soon as it‚Äôs reopening it brought back a lot of memories for myself as well as my fellow Cal alumni. As an undergrad I still remember Mezzo was a lot smaller in size and and most of us would sit along a railing to eat our salad. It definitely is a great place to reminisce and to enjoy.< /review>

YUM!!! My friend took me to this place when I visited and it was so good! Super cute, casual shop. Super clean interior and spacious. <Text>Warning: service here is super variable. If you order the same thing every time, you will undoubtedly get a different sandwich each time (in regards to quantity of ingredients, how the sandwich is put together). People enjoy the big portions here, but when someone skimps on your sandwich ingredients, it doesn't feel like a lot. Sometimes this inconsistency works in your favor, often times not. Overall though, the inconsistency is frustrating. I've ordered a BLTA to-go here and when I got home, I found no avocados... I mean... it's in the name! Generally, the BLTA is pretty good, lots of different components: sprouts, peppers, spicy mayo, crispy thick bacon, good tomatoes, and plenty of avocado slices (if they don't forget them or skimp). Bread is good, in particular I enjoyed the cheese jalapeno roll.

The soup is alright (Thai chicken and rice) but the chicken was a bit tough and chewy. Mint coffee is interesting as well, pretty good. Pastries are alright.

Overall, this place is okay. Service is fairly quick but the line can get horrifically long. At those times, it is definitely not worth the wait, in my opinion.<//Text>< Pictures>

<time>1565363854846<//time><Rate>5</Rate>< Review>
I was a regular in the previous incarnation of Mezzo, back in the 90s, and couldn't get enough of their immense salads and hearty hummus sandwiches. I don't live in the area anymore, but whenever I visit I am drawn to Mezzo. The food is just like I remember it. A half sandwich and green salad could be skimpy in another restaurant, but here at Mezzo you're getting a generously filled sandwich -- you have to try their amazing honey wheat bread -- and not just a typical "side salad" but a full-fledged salad bowl with lettuce, cherry tomatoes, veggies, and croutons. So satisfying!

The old place was a little claustrophobic and known for unfriendly service, but now they have more space and a much nicer staff. They're doing something right! I hope they're around for years to come.< /Review>
